30 /*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
31  MODULE DEFINITION FOR MULTIPLE INCLUSION
32 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
33 #ifndef STLUX_STNRG_H
34 #define STLUX_STNRG_H
35 
36 /* Check the used compiler */
37 #if defined(__CSMC__)
38  #define _COSMIC_
39 #elif defined(__RCST7__)
40  #define _RAISONANCE_
41 #elif defined(__ICCSTM8__)
42  #define _IAR_
43 #elif defined(__SDCC)
44  #define _SDCC_
45  #define SDCC_VERSION (__SDCC_VERSION_MAJOR * 10000 \
46  + __SDCC_VERSION_MINOR * 100 \
47  + __SDCC_VERSION_PATCH)
48 #else
49  #error in 'STLUX_STNRG.h': compiler not supported
50 #endif

52 
53 /*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
54  MEMORY WIDTH
55 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
56 
57 // if memory sizes [B] are not given, assume smallest available in family
58 #if !defined(STM8_PFLASH_SIZE)
59  #warning undefined STM8_PFLASH_SIZE, assume minimum
60  #define STM8_PFLASH_SIZE 32768 ///< size of program flash [B]
61 #endif
62 #if !defined(STM8_RAM_SIZE)
63  #warning undefined STM8_RAM_SIZE, assume minimum
64  #define STM8_RAM_SIZE 2048 ///< size of RAM [B]
65 #endif
66 #if !defined(STM8_EEPROM_SIZE)
67  #warning undefined STM8_EEPROM_SIZE, assume minimum
68  #define STM8_EEPROM_SIZE 1024 ///< size of data EEPROM [B]
69 #endif
70 
71 // memory start / end addresses
72 #define STM8_PFLASH_START 0x8000 ///< first address in program flash
73 #define STM8_PFLASH_END (STM8_PFLASH_START + STM8_PFLASH_SIZE - 1) ///< last address in program flash
74 #define STM8_RAM_START 0x0000 ///< first address in RAM
75 #define STM8_RAM_END (STM8_RAM_START + STM8_RAM_SIZE - 1) ///< last address in RAM
76 #define STM8_EEPROM_START 0x4000 ///< first address in EEPROM
77 #define STM8_EEPROM_END (STM8_EEPROM_START + STM8_EEPROM_SIZE - 1) ///< last address in EEPROM (part of P-flash, configure via option byte)
78 
79 // address space width (>32kB flash exceeds 16bit, as flash starts at 0x8000)
80 #if (STM8_PFLASH_END <= 0xFFFF)
81  #define STM8_ADDR_WIDTH 16 ///< width of address space
82  #define STM8_MEM_POINTER_T uint16_t ///< address variable type
83 #else
84  #define STM8_ADDR_WIDTH 32 ///< width of address space
85  #define STM8_MEM_POINTER_T uint32_t ///< address variable type
86 #endif
87 
88 
89 /*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
90  COMPILER SPECIFIC SETTINGS
91 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
92 
93 // Cosmic compiler
94 #if defined(_COSMIC_)
95 
96  // macros to unify ISR declaration and implementation
97  #define ISR_HANDLER(func,irq) @far @interrupt void func(void) ///< handler for interrupt service routine
98  #define ISR_HANDLER_TRAP(func) void @far @interrupt func(void) ///< handler for trap service routine
99 
100  // common assembler instructions
101  #define NOP() _asm("nop") ///< perform a nop() operation (=minimum delay)
102  #define DISABLE_INTERRUPTS() _asm("sim") ///< disable interrupt handling
103  #define ENABLE_INTERRUPTS() _asm("rim") ///< enable interrupt handling
104  #define TRIGGER_TRAP _asm("trap") ///< trigger a trap (=soft interrupt) e.g. for EMC robustness (see AN1015)
105  #define WAIT_FOR_INTERRUPT() _asm("wfi") ///< stop code execution and wait for interrupt
106  #define ENTER_HALT() _asm("halt") ///< put controller to HALT mode
107  #define SW_RESET() (_WWDG_CR = _WWDG_CR_WDGA) ///< reset controller via WWDG module
108 
109  // data type in bit fields
110  #define _BITS unsigned int ///< data type in bit structs (follow C90 standard)
111 
112 // Raisonance Compiler
113 #elif defined(_RAISONANCE_)
114 
115  // include intrinsic functions
116  #include <intrins.h>
117 
118  // macros to unify ISR declaration and implementation
119  #define ISR_HANDLER(func,irq) void func(void) interrupt irq ///< handler for interrupt service routine
120  #define ISR_HANDLER_TRAP(func) void func(void) trap ///< handler for trap service routine
121 
122  // common assembler instructions
123  #define NOP() _nop_() ///< perform a nop() operation (=minimum delay)
124  #define DISABLE_INTERRUPTS() _sim_() ///< disable interrupt handling
125  #define ENABLE_INTERRUPTS() _rim_() ///< enable interrupt handling
126  #define TRIGGER_TRAP _trap_() ///< trigger a trap (=soft interrupt) e.g. for EMC robustness (see AN1015)
127  #define WAIT_FOR_INTERRUPT() _wfi_() ///< stop code execution and wait for interrupt
128  #define ENTER_HALT() _halt_() ///< put controller to HALT mode
129  #define SW_RESET() (_WWDG_CR = _WWDG_CR_WDGA) ///< reset controller via WWDG module
130 
131  // data type in bit fields
132  #define _BITS unsigned int ///< data type in bit structs (follow C90 standard)
133 
134 // IAR Compiler
135 #elif defined(_IAR_)
136 input mo
137  // include intrinsic functions
138  #include <intrinsics.h>
139 
140  // macros to unify ISR declaration and implementation
141  #define ISR_HANDLER(func,irq) __interrupt void func(void) ///< handler for interrupt service routine
142  //#define ISR_HANDLER_TRAP(func) void func(void) trap ///< handler for trap service routine
143 
144  // common assembler instructions
145  #define NOP() __no_operation() ///< perform a nop() operation (=minimum delay)
146  #define DISABLE_INTERRUPTS() __disable_interrupt() ///< disable interrupt handling
147  #define ENABLE_INTERRUPTS() __enable_interrupt() ///< enable interrupt handling
148  #define TRIGGER_TRAP __trap() ///< trigger a trap (=soft interrupt) e.g. for EMC robustness (see AN1015)
149  #define WAIT_FOR_INTERRUPT() __wait_for_interrupt() ///< stop code execution and wait for interrupt
150  #define ENTER_HALT() __halt() ///< put controller to HALT mode
151  #define SW_RESET() (_WWDG_CR = _WWDG_CR_WDGA) ///< reset controller via WWDG module
152 
153  // data type in bit fields
154  #define _BITS unsigned char ///< data type in bit structs (deviating from C90 standard)
155 
156 // SDCC compiler
157 #elif defined(_SDCC_)
158 
159  // macros to unify ISR declaration and implementation
160  #define ISR_HANDLER(func,irq) void func(void) __interrupt(irq) ///< handler for interrupt service routine
161  #if SDCC_VERSION >= 30403 // traps require >=v3.4.3
162  #define ISR_HANDLER_TRAP(func) void func() __trap ///< handler for trap service routine
163  #else
164  #error traps require SDCC >=3.4.3. Please update!
165  #endif
166 
167  // common assembler instructions
168  #define NOP() __asm__("nop") ///< perform a nop() operation (=minimum delay)
169  #define DISABLE_INTERRUPTS() __asm__("sim") ///< disable interrupt handling
170  #define ENABLE_INTERRUPTS() __asm__("rim") ///< enable interrupt handling
171  #define TRIGGER_TRAP __asm__("trap") ///< trigger a trap (=soft interrupt) e.g. for EMC robustness (see AN1015)
172  #define WAIT_FOR_INTERRUPT() __asm__("wfi") ///< stop code execution and wait for interrupt
173  #define ENTER_HALT() __asm__("halt") ///< put controller to HALT mode
174  #define SW_RESET() (_WWDG_CR = _WWDG_CR_WDGA) ///< reset controller via WWDG module
175 
176  // data type in bit fields
177  #define _BITS unsigned int ///< data type in bit structs (follow C90 standard)
178 
179 #endif

182 /*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
183  DEFINITION OF GLOBAL MACROS/#DEFINES
184 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
185 
186 // general macros
187 #define _SFR(type, addr) (*((volatile type*) (addr))) ///< peripheral register
188 #if defined(_DOXYGEN) || defined(UID_AddressBase)
189  #define _UID(N) _SFR(uint8_t, UID_AddressBase+N) ///< read unique identifier byte N
190 #endif
191 #if defined(_DOXYGEN) || defined(DEVID_AddressBase)
192  #define _DEVID(N) _SFR(uint8_t, DEVID_AddressBase+N) ///< read device identifier byte N
193 #endif

196 /*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
197  STANDARD DATA TYPES
198 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
199 #if defined(_COSMIC_) || defined(_RAISONANCE_) || defined(_IAR_)
200 
201  // skip if already defined
202  #ifndef INT8_MAX
203 
204  // compiler specific --> If possible, use <stdint.h> from compiler
205  typedef signed long int32_t;
206  typedef signed short int16_t;
207  typedef signed char int8_t;
208 
209  typedef unsigned long uint32_t;
210  typedef unsigned short uint16_t;
211  typedef unsigned char uint8_t;
212 
213 
214  // define min/max values
215  #define INT8_MAX 0x7f
216  #define INT8_MIN (-INT8_MAX - 1)
217 
218  #define UINT8_MAX 0xFF
219  #define UINT8_MIN 0
220 
221  #define INT16_MAX 0x7fff
222  #define INT16_MIN (-INT16_MAX - 1)
223 
224  #define UINT16_MAX 0xFFFF
225  #define UINT16_MIN 0
226 
227  #define INT32_MAX 0x7fffffffL
228  #define INT32_MIN (-INT32_MAX - 1L)
229 
230  #define UINT32_MAX 0xFFFFFFFF
231  #define UINT32_MIN 0
232 
233  #endif // INT8_MAX
234 
235 #elif defined(_SDCC_)
236 
237  // use compiler header
238  #include <stdint.h>
239 
240 #endif

243 /*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
244  ISR Vector Table (SDCC, Raisonance, IAR)
245  Note: IAR has an IRQ offset of +2 compared to STM8 datasheet (see below)
246 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
247 
248 // reserved 0
249 #define __AWU_VECTOR__ 1 ///< irq1 - Auto Wake Up from Halt interrupt (AWU)
250 #define __CLK_VECTOR__ 2 ///< irq2 - Clock controller interrupt
251 #define __PORT0_VECTOR__ 3 ///< irq3 - External interrupt port 0
252 #define __AUXTIM_VECTOR__ 4 ///< irq4 - Auxiliary timer interrupt
253 #define __PORT2_VECTOR__ 5 ///< irq5 - External interrupt port 2
254 #define __SMED0_VECTOR__ 6 ///< irq6 - SMED-0 interrupt
255 #define __SMED1_VECTOR__ 7 ///< irq7 - SMED-1 control logic interrupt
256 // reserved 8
257 // reserved 9
258 // reserved 10
259 // reserved 11
260 // reserved 12
261 // reserved 13
262 // reserved 14
263 #define __SMED2_VECTOR__ 15 ///< irq15 - SMED-2 control logic interrupt
264 #define __SMED3_VECTOR__ 16 ///< irq16 - SMED-3 control logic interrupt
265 #define __UART_TXE_VECTOR__ 17 ///< irq17 - UART send (TX empty) interrupt
266 #define __UART_RXF_VECTOR__ 18 ///< irq18 - UART receive (RX full) interrupt
267 #define __I2C_VECTOR__ 19 ///< irq19 - I2C interrupt
268 // reserved 20
269 // reserved 21
270 #define __ADC_VECTOR__ 22 ///< irq22 - ADC end of conversion interrupt
271 #define __SYSTIM_UPD_OVF_VECTOR__ 23 ///< irq23 - system timer Update/overflow interrupt
272 #define __FLASH_VECTOR__ 24 ///< irq24 - flash interrupt
273 #define __DALI_VECTOR__ 25 ///< irq25 - DALI interrupt line
274 #define __SMED4_VECTOR__ 26 ///< irq26 - SMED-3 control logic interrupt
275 #define __SMED5_VECTOR__ 27 ///< irq27 - SMED-4 control logic interrupt
276 // reserved 28
277 // reserved 29

280 /*-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
281  DEFINITION OF STM8 PERIPHERAL REGISTERS
282 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
283 
284 //------------------------
285 // General purpose input/output pins (_PORT)
286 //------------------------
287 #if defined(_DOXYGEN) || defined(PORT0_AddressBase) || defined(PORT1_AddressBase)
288 
289  /** @brief structure for controlling pins in port mode (_PORTx, x=0..1) */
290  typedef struct {
291 
292  /** @brief PORTx output data register (_PORTx_ODR) */
293  struct {
294  _BITS PIN0 : 1; ///< pin 0 output control
295  _BITS PIN1 : 1; ///< pin 1 output control
296  _BITS PIN2 : 1; ///< pin 2 output control
297  _BITS PIN3 : 1; ///< pin 3 output control
298  _BITS PIN4 : 1; ///< pin 4 output control
299  _BITS PIN5 : 1; ///< pin 5 output control
300  _BITS PIN6 : 1; ///< pin 6 output control
301  _BITS PIN7 : 1; ///< pin 7 output control
302  } ODR;
303 
304  /** @brief PORTx input data register (_PORTx_IDR) */
305  struct {
306  _BITS PIN0 : 1; ///< pin 0 input control
307  _BITS PIN1 : 1; ///< pin 1 input control
308  _BITS PIN2 : 1; ///< pin 2 input control
309  _BITS PIN3 : 1; ///< pin 3 input control
310  _BITS PIN4 : 1; ///< pin 4 input control
311  _BITS PIN5 : 1; ///< pin 5 input control
312  _BITS PIN6 : 1; ///< pin 6 input control
313  _BITS PIN7 : 1; ///< pin 7 input control
314  } IDR;
315 
316  /** @brief PORTx data direction data register (_PORTx_DDR) */
317  struct {
318  _BITS PIN0 : 1; ///< pin 0 direction control
319  _BITS PIN1 : 1; ///< pin 1 direction control
320  _BITS PIN2 : 1; ///< pin 2 direction control
321  _BITS PIN3 : 1; ///< pin 3 direction control
322  _BITS PIN4 : 1; ///< pin 4 direction control
323  _BITS PIN5 : 1; ///< pin 5 direction control
324  _BITS PIN6 : 1; ///< pin 6 direction control
325  _BITS PIN7 : 1; ///< pin 7 direction control
326  } DDR;
327 
328  /** @brief PORTx control register 1 (_PORTx_CR1) */
329  struct {
330  _BITS PIN0 : 1; ///< pin 0 control register 1
331  _BITS PIN1 : 1; ///< pin 1 control register 1
332  _BITS PIN2 : 1; ///< pin 2 control register 1
333  _BITS PIN3 : 1; ///< pin 3 control register 1
334  _BITS PIN4 : 1; ///< pin 4 control register 1
335  _BITS PIN5 : 1; ///< pin 5 control register 1
336  _BITS PIN6 : 1; ///< pin 6 control register 1
337  _BITS PIN7 : 1; ///< pin 7 control register 1
338  } CR1;
339 
340  /** @brief PORTx control register 1 (_PORTx_CR2) */
341  struct {
342  _BITS PIN0 : 1; ///< pin 0 control register 2
343  _BITS PIN1 : 1; ///< pin 1 control register 2
344  _BITS PIN2 : 1; ///< pin 2 control register 2
345  _BITS PIN3 : 1; ///< pin 3 control register 2
346  _BITS PIN4 : 1; ///< pin 4 control register 2
347  _BITS PIN5 : 1; ///< pin 5 control register 2
348  _BITS PIN6 : 1; ///< pin 6 control register 2
349  _BITS PIN7 : 1; ///< pin 7 control register 2
350  } CR2;
351 
352  } _PORT_t;
353 
354  /* Pointer to PORT0 registers */
355  #if defined(PORT0_AddressBase)
356  #define _PORT0 _SFR(_PORT_t, PORT0_AddressBase) ///< PORT0 struct/bit access
357  #define _PORT0_ODR _SFR(uint8_t, PORT0_AddressBase+0x00) ///< PORT0 output register
358  #define _PORT0_IDR _SFR(uint8_t, PORT0_AddressBase+0x01) ///< PORT0 input register
359  #define _PORT0_DDR _SFR(uint8_t, PORT0_AddressBase+0x02) ///< PORT0 direction register
360  #define _PORT0_CR1 _SFR(uint8_t, PORT0_AddressBase+0x03) ///< PORT0 control register 1
361  #define _PORT0_CR2 _SFR(uint8_t, PORT0_AddressBase+0x04) ///< PORT0 control register 2
362  #endif
363 
364  /* Pointer to PORT1 registers */
365  #if defined(PORT1_AddressBase)
366  #define _PORT1 _SFR(_PORT_t, PORT1_AddressBase) ///< PORT1 struct/bit access
367  #define _PORT1_ODR _SFR(uint8_t, PORT1_AddressBase+0x00) ///< PORT1 output register
368  #define _PORT1_IDR _SFR(uint8_t, PORT1_AddressBase+0x01) ///< PORT1 input register
369  #define _PORT1_DDR _SFR(uint8_t, PORT1_AddressBase+0x02) ///< PORT1 direction register
370  #define _PORT1_CR1 _SFR(uint8_t, PORT1_AddressBase+0x03) ///< PORT1 control register 1
371  #define _PORT1_CR2 _SFR(uint8_t, PORT1_AddressBase+0x04) ///< PORT1 control register 2
372  #endif
373 
374 
375  /* PORT Module Reset Values (all ports) */
376  #define _PORT_ODR_RESET_VALUE ((uint8_t) 0x00) ///< PORTx output register reset value
377  #define _PORT_DDR_RESET_VALUE ((uint8_t) 0x00) ///< PORTx direction register reset value
378  #define _PORT_CR1_RESET_VALUE ((uint8_t) 0x00) ///< PORTx control register 1 reset value
379  #define _PORT_CR2_RESET_VALUE ((uint8_t) 0x00) ///< PORTx control register 2 reset value
380 
381 
382  /* macro for accessing pin registers (all ports) */
383  #define _PORT_PIN0 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 0)) ///< PORTx bit mask for pin 0 (in _PORTx_ODR, _PORTx_IDR, _PORTx_DDR, _PORTx_CR1, _PORTx_CR2)
384  #define _PORT_PIN1 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 1)) ///< PORTx bit mask for pin 1 (in _PORTx_ODR, _PORTx_IDR, _PORTx_DDR, _PORTx_CR1, _PORTx_CR2)
385  #define _PORT_PIN2 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 2)) ///< PORTx bit mask for pin 2 (in _PORTx_ODR, _PORTx_IDR, _PORTx_DDR, _PORTx_CR1, _PORTx_CR2)
386  #define _PORT_PIN3 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 3)) ///< PORTx bit mask for pin 3 (in _PORTx_ODR, _PORTx_IDR, _PORTx_DDR, _PORTx_CR1, _PORTx_CR2)
387  #define _PORT_PIN4 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 4)) ///< PORTx bit mask for pin 4 (in _PORTx_ODR, _PORTx_IDR, _PORTx_DDR, _PORTx_CR1, _PORTx_CR2)
388  #define _PORT_PIN5 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 5)) ///< PORTx bit mask for pin 5 (in _PORTx_ODR, _PORTx_IDR, _PORTx_DDR, _PORTx_CR1, _PORTx_CR2)
389  #define _PORT_PIN6 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 6)) ///< PORTx bit mask for pin 6 (in _PORTx_ODR, _PORTx_IDR, _PORTx_DDR, _PORTx_CR1, _PORTx_CR2)
390  #define _PORT_PIN7 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 7)) ///< PORTx bit mask for pin 7 (in _PORTx_ODR, _PORTx_IDR, _PORTx_DDR, _PORTx_CR1, _PORTx_CR2)
391 
392 #endif // PORTx_AddressBase

401  /** @brief struct for miscellaneous direct register access (_MSC) */
402  typedef struct {
403 
404  /** @brief port 0 interrupt control 0 (_MSC_CFGP00) */
405  struct {
406  _BITS INT_LEV : 1; ///< interrupt request active level
407  _BITS INT_SEL : 2; ///< interrupt source configuration
408  _BITS INT_ENB : 1; ///< interrupt enable
409  _BITS INT_TYPE : 1; ///< interrupt type configuration IRQ/NMI
410  _BITS : 3; // Reserved, must be kept clear
411  } CFGP00;
412 
413

419  _BITS INT_TYPE : 1; ///< interrupt type configuration IRQ/NMI
420  _BITS : 3; // Reserved, must be kept clear
421  } CFGP01;

524  /** @brief port 0 interrupt status (_MSC_STSP0) */
525  struct {
526  _BITS INT_0 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port0[0] or timer 0
527  _BITS INT_1 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port0[1] or timer 1
528  _BITS INT_2 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port0[2]
529  _BITS INT_3 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port0[3]
530  _BITS INT_4 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port0[4]
531  _BITS INT_5 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port0[5] or CCO aux timer
532  _BITS : 2; // Reserved, must be kept clear
533  } STSP0;
534 
535 
536  /** @brief port 2 interrupt status (_MSC_STSP2) */
537  struct {
538  _BITS INT_0 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port2[0] or timer 0
539  _BITS INT_1 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port2[1] or timer 1
540  _BITS INT_2 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port2[2]
541  _BITS INT_3 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port2[3]
542  _BITS INT_4 : 1; ///< interrupt pending for port2[4]

1058  /* Pointer to flash registers */
1059  #define _MSC _SFR(_MSC_t, MSC_AddressBase) ///< MSC misc register struct/bit access
1060  #define _MSC_CFGP00 _SFR(uint8_t, MSC_AddressBase+0x00) ///< MSC port 0 interrupt control 0
1061  #define _MSC_CFGP01 _SFR(uint8_t, MSC_AddressBase+0x01) ///< MSC port 0 interrupt control 1
1062  #define _MSC_CFGP02 _SFR(uint8_t, MSC_AddressBase+0x02) ///< MSC port 0 interrupt control 2

1362  /** @brief struct to control write/erase of flash memory (_FLASH) */

1369  _BITS AHALT : 1; ///< Power-down in Active-halt mode
1370  _BITS HALT : 1; ///< Power-down in Halt mode
1371  _BITS : 4; // Reserved
1372  } CR1;
1373

1376  struct {
1377  _BITS PRG : 1; ///< Standard block programming
1378  _BITS : 3; // Reserved
1379  _BITS FPRG : 1; ///< Fast block programming
1380  _BITS ERASE : 1; ///< Block erasing
1381  _BITS WPRG : 1; ///< Word programming
1382  _BITS OPT : 1; ///< Write option bytes
1383  } CR2;
1384

1387  struct {
1388  _BITS NPRG : 1; ///< Standard block programming
1389  _BITS : 3; // Reserved

1391  _BITS NERASE : 1; ///< Block erasing
1392  _BITS NWPRG : 1; ///< Word programming
1393  _BITS NOPT : 1; ///< Write option bytes
1394  } NCR2;
1395 
1396

1413  _BITS EOP : 1; ///< End of programming (write or erase operation) flag
1414  _BITS DUL : 1; ///< Data EEPROM area unlocked flag
1415  _BITS : 2; // Reserved, forced by hardware to 0
1416  _BITS HVOFF : 1; ///< End of high voltage flag
1417  _BITS : 1; // Reserved
1418  } IAPSR;

1726  _BITS CCOBSY : 1; ///< Configurable clock output busy
1727  _BITS : 1; // Reserved, must be kept cleared.
1728  } CCOR;

2460  _BITS DIV_12_15 : 4; ///< UART_DIV [15:12]
2461  } BRR2;
2462 
2463 
2464  /** @brief UART Control register 1 (_UART_CR1) */
2465  struct {
2466  _BITS PIEN : 1; ///< Parity interrupt enable
2467  _BITS PS : 1; ///< Parity selection
2468  _BITS PCEN : 1; ///< Parity control enable
2469  _BITS WAKE : 1; ///< Wakeup method
2470  _BITS M : 1; ///< word length
2471  _BITS UARTD : 1; ///< UART Disable (for low power consumption)
2472  _BITS T8 : 1; ///< Transmit Data bit 8 (in 9-bit mode)
2473  _BITS R8 : 1; ///< Receive Data bit 8 (in 9-bit mode)
2474  } CR1;
2475 
2476 
2477  /** @brief UART Control register 2 (_UART_CR2) */
2478  struct {
2479  _BITS SBK : 1; ///< Send break
2480  _BITS RWU : 1; ///< Receiver wakeup
2481  _BITS REN : 1; ///< Receiver enable
2482  _BITS TEN : 1; ///< Transmitter enable
2483  _BITS ILIEN : 1; ///< IDLE Line interrupt enable
2484  _BITS RIEN : 1; ///< Receiver interrupt enable
2485  _BITS TCIEN : 1; ///< Transmission complete interrupt enable
2486  _BITS TIEN : 1; ///< Transmitter interrupt enable
2487  } CR2;
2488 
2489

2491  struct {
2492  _BITS : 4; // Reserved
2493  _BITS STOP : 2; ///< STOP bits
2494  _BITS : 2; // Reserved
2495  } CR3;
2496

2500  _BITS ADD : 4; ///< Address of the UART node
2501  _BITS : 4; // Reserved
2502  } CR4;
2503 
2504  } _UART_t;

2536  #define _UART_SR_TXE ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 7)) ///< UART Transmit data register empty [0]

2539  #define _UART_CR1_PIEN ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 0)) ///< UART Parity interrupt enable [0]
2540  #define _UART_CR1_PS ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 1)) ///< UART Parity selection [0]
2541  #define _UART_CR1_PCEN ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 2)) ///< UART Parity control enable [0]
2542  #define _UART_CR1_WAKE ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 3)) ///< UART Wakeup method [0]
2543  #define _UART_CR1_M ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 4)) ///< UART word length [0]
2544  #define _UART_CR1_UARTD ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 5)) ///< UART Disable (for low power consumption) [0]
2545  #define _UART_CR1_T8 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 6)) ///< UART Transmit Data bit 8 (in 9-bit mode) [0]
2546  #define _UART_CR1_R8 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 7)) ///< UART Receive Data bit 8 (in 9-bit mode) [0]

2556  #define _UART_CR2_TIEN ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 7)) ///< UART Transmitter interrupt enable [0]

2563  // reserved [7:6]
2564

2570  #define _UART_CR4_ADD3 ((uint8_t) (0x01 << 3)) ///< UART Address of the UART node [3]

3340  /** @brief SMEDn Interrupt request register (_SMEDn_IRQ) */
3341  struct {
3342  _BITS CNT_OVER : 1; ///< counter overflow interrupt request
3343  _BITS EXT0_INT : 1; ///< InSig[0] capture interrupt request
3344  _BITS EXT1_INT : 1; ///< InSig[1] capture interrupt request
3345  _BITS EXT2_INT : 1; ///< InSig[2] capture interrupt request
3346  _BITS STA_S0_IT : 1; ///< Tmr(0) transition interrupt request
3347  _BITS STA_S1_IT : 1; ///< Tmr(1) transition interrupt request
3348  _BITS STA_S2_IT : 1; ///< Tmr(2) transition interrupt request
3349  _BITS STA_S3_IT : 1; ///< Tmr(3) transition interrupt request
3350  } IRQ;
3351 
3352  /** @brief SMEDn Interrupt enable register (_SMEDn_IER) */
3353  struct {
3354  _BITS CNT_OV_E : 1; ///< counter overflow interrupt enable
3355  _BITS IT_EN_EX0 : 1; ///< InSig[0] capture interrupt enable
3356  _BITS IT_EN_EX1 : 1; ///< InSig[1] capture interrupt enable
3357  _BITS IT_EN_EX2 : 1; ///< InSig[2] capture interrupt enable
3358  _BITS IT_STA_S0 : 1; ///< Tmr(0) transition interrupt enable
3359  _BITS IT_STA_S1 : 1; ///< Tmr(1) transition interrupt enable
3360  _BITS IT_STA_S2 : 1; ///< Tmr(2) transition interrupt enable
3361  _BITS IT_STA_S3 : 1; ///< Tmr(3) transition interrupt enable
3362  } IER;
3363 
3364  /** @brief SMEDn External event control register (_SMEDn_ISEL) */
3365  struct {
3366  _BITS INPUT0_EN : 1; ///< InSig[0] input enable
3367  _BITS INPUT1_EN : 1; ///< InSig[1] input enable
3368  _BITS INPUT2_EN : 1; ///< InSig[2] input enable
3369  _BITS INPUT_LAT : 1; ///< enable latch function on InSig[0] input
3370  _BITS : 4; // Reserved, must be kept clear
3371  } ISEL;
3372 
3373  /** @brief SMEDn Dump enable register (_SMEDn_DMP) */
3374  struct {
3375  _BITS DMPE_EX0 : 1; ///< dump update mode for InSig[0] event
3376  _BITS DMPE_EX1 : 1; ///< dump update mode for InSig[1] event
3377  _BITS DMPE_EX2 : 1; ///< dump update mode for InSig[2] event
3378  _BITS DMP_EVER : 1; ///< dump update mode all
3379  _BITS CPL_IT_GE : 1; ///< lock together SMEDn_GSTS and SMEDn_IRQ reset signal
3380  _BITS : 3; // Reserved, must be kept clear
3381  } DMP;
3382 
3383  /** @brief SMEDn finite state machine status register (_SMEDn_FSM_STS) */
3384  struct {
3385  _BITS FSM : 3; ///< finite state machine state variable
3386  _BITS PWM : 1; ///< PWM output signal
3387  _BITS EVINP : 3; ///< event input signals
3388  _BITS : 1; // Reserved, must be kept clear
3389  } FSM_STS;
3390 
3391  } _SMED_t;
3392
